57

59	        >>> controlnet = ControlNetModel.from_pretrained("lllyasviel/sd-controlnet-canny", torch_dtype=torch.float16)
60	        >>> pipe = StableDiffusionControlNetPipeline.from_pretrained(
61	        ...     "runwayml/stable-diffusion-v1-5", controlnet=controlnet, torch_dtype=torch.float16
62	        ... )
63	
64	        >>> # speed up diffusion process with faster scheduler and memory optimization
65	        >>> pipe.scheduler = UniPCMultistepScheduler.from_config(pipe.scheduler.config)
66	        >>> # remove following line if xformers is not installed
67	        >>> pipe.enable_xformers_memory_efficient_attention()
68	
69	        >>> pipe.enable_model_cpu_offload()
70	
71	        >>> # generate image
72	        >>> generator = torch.manual_seed(0)
73	        >>> image = pipe(
74	        ...     "futuristic-looking woman", num_inference_steps=20, generator=generator, image=canny_image
